# 1. Cifar10

```{.python .input  n=7}
dataset_name = 'cifar10'
(x_train, y_train), (x_test, y_test), (input_shape, num_classes) = load_keras_dataset(
    dataset_name, model_type='cnn'
)
```

```{.json .output n=7}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "x_train shape: (50000, 3, 32, 32)\ny_train shape: (50000, 1)\n50000 train samples\n10000 test samples\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=22}
x_sub, y_sub = down_sampling(x_test, y_test)
x_rescaled, input_shape = batch_rescale(x_sub, 10.0)
```

```{.python .input  n=23}
input_shape
```

```{.python .input  n=13}
encoder = ResNet50(input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False,
                   weights='imagenet', pooling='max')
```

```{.python .input  n=16}
%%time
z = encoder.predict_generator(x_rescaled, steps=1000, workers=1)
```

```{.python .input  n=17}
pca = PCA(n_components=2).fit(z)
fig = visualize_feature(pca, z, y_sub[:, 0], markersize=128)
display(fig)
```

# 2. FashionMNIST

```{.python .input  n=2}
dataset_name = 'fashion_mnist'
(x_train, y_train), (x_test, y_test), (input_shape, num_classes) = load_keras_dataset(
    dataset_name, model_type='cnn'
)
```

```{.json .output n=2}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "x_train shape: (60000, 1, 28, 28)\ny_train shape: (60000,)\n60000 train samples\n10000 test samples\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=15}
x_sub, y_sub = down_sampling(x_test, y_test)
x_rescaled, input_shape = batch_rescale(x_sub, scale=10.0, to_3ch=True)
```

```{.python .input  n=4}
encoder = ResNet50(input_shape=input_shape, include_top=False,
                   weights='imagenet', pooling='max')
```

```{.python .input  n=16}
%%time
z = encoder.predict_generator(x_rescaled, steps=1000, workers=1)
```

```{.json .output n=16}
[
 {
  "name": "stdout",
  "output_type": "stream",
  "text": "CPU times: user 30.1 s, sys: 18.8 s, total: 48.8 s\nWall time: 44.5 s\n"
 }
]
```

```{.python .input  n=18}
pca = PCA(n_components=2).fit(z)
fig = visualize_feature(pca, z, y_sub, xlim=[-2, 2], ylim=[-2, 2], markersize=128)
display(fig)
```
